> 19–21. **"Indeed man was created `halū'an` (restless, anxious, impatient) — when evil touches him he is distressed (`jazū'an`) — when good touches him he is withholding (`manū'an`)"**

**Ayat 22–35: The exception-profile:**
> 22–35. **"Except those who pray — who are constant in their prayer — in whose wealth there is a known right for the beggar and the deprived — who believe in the Day of Judgment — who fear the punishment of their Lord — who guard their private parts — who honor their trusts and covenants — who stand upright in their testimonies — who are careful of their prayer"**

**Ayat 36–41: Those who rush from the right and left:**
> 36–41. Groups rushing in from every side to receive — every person seeking to enter the Garden — "No! indeed We created them from what they know" — by the Lord of every rising — We are certainly capable of replacing them with better than them

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayah 4: Fifty-thousand-year Day** | The Day's duration is fifty thousand years. This is the scale of accountability — not a moment, not a day. The source's management of the Day's proceedings requires an interval of time that dwarfs all of human history. The soul that tries to imagine the Day using dunya-timescales cannot comprehend what awaits. |
| **Ayat 19–21: Halū'an — the default of anxious-impatience** | Man's baseline is `halū'`: restless, anxious, impatient. When evil hits → distressed (`jazū'`). When good arrives → hoarding (`manū'`). This is the unmodified human response pattern: react with anxiety to difficulty, react with stinginess to abundance. Both responses are defaults, not choices — they are structural until redirected by faith-practice. |
| **Ayat 22–35: The exception-architecture** | The exception to the halū' default is not a single act but a cluster of ongoing practices: prayer-constancy + known-right-in-wealth + Day-belief + fear-of-punishment + chastity-guarding + trusts + testimonies + prayer-carefulness. The entire exception-profile is structured the same way as Al-Mu'minūn's believer-profile: ongoing present-states, not one-time actions. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Halū' baseline: the default human pattern is anxiety-in-difficulty + stinginess-in-abundance — redirected only by consistent practice | ❌ Missing |
| Exception-architecture: the override of human defaults requires a cluster of ongoing practices working simultaneously | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 80 — Surah Al-Nabā' (78) — The Great News; about what are they asking each other? — about the great news about which they differ; have We not made the earth a resting place and the mountains as stakes; We created you in pairs; We made your sleep for rest; We made the day for livelihood; We built above you seven strong ones; the Day the trumpet is blown; Hell is lying in wait; the Gardens of Paradise for the righteous; that is the Day of account — "My Lord — I wish I had been dust".*

---

### REVELATION 80 — SURAH AL-NABĀ' (78), ALL 40 AYAT
*The Great News — the disputed Great News; eight creation-sign pairs; the Day the trumpet blows; Hell as lying-in-wait (`mirṣādā`); the Merciful's permission required to speak on that Day; the disbeliever's wish to be dust.*

---

**Ayat 1–5: The disputed Great News:**
> 1–5. **"`'Amma yatasā'alūn` — about what are they asking each other? — about the Great News (`al-naba' al-'aẓīm`) — about which they differ — no — they will know — no — they will know"**

**Ayat 6–16: Eight paired creation-signs:**
> 6–16. "Have We not made the earth a resting place (`mihādā`) — and the mountains as stakes (`awtādā`) — We created you in pairs (`azwājā`) — We made your sleep as rest (`subātā`) — We made the night as a covering (`libāsā`) — We made the day for livelihood (`ma'āshā`) — We built above you seven strong ones (`shidādā`) — We made a blazing lamp — We sent down from rain-clouds pouring water — to produce grain and vegetation and dense gardens"

**Ayat 17–20: The Day's opening:**
> 17–20. **"Indeed the Day of Decision is an appointed time — the Day the trumpet is blown and you come in crowds (`afwājā`) — the sky is opened and becomes gateways — the mountains are moved and become a mirage"**

**Ayah 21: Hell as lying-in-wait:**
> 21–22. **"Indeed Hell has been lying in wait (`mirṣādā`) — a return-place for the transgressors"**

**Ayah 37–38: The Merciful's permission to speak:**
> 37–38. **"The Lord of the heavens and earth and what is between them — the Most Merciful — they have no power to address Him (`lā yamlikūna minhu khiṭābā`) — the Day the Spirit and the angels stand in rows — they do not speak except for one whom the Most Merciful permits — and he will speak only what is correct"**

**Ayah 40: The dust-wish:**
> 40. **"Indeed We have warned you of an imminent punishment — the Day a man sees what his hands have put forth — and the disbeliever says: `yā laytanī kuntu turābā` — O I wish I had been dust"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayat 6–16: Eight creation-pairs as witnesses** | The eight creation-signs are all paired opposites that form working systems: earth/mountains (resting/anchoring), sleep/day (rest/activity), night/light-lamp (covering/illuminating), pairs/rain (reproduction/nourishment). Each pair is a balanced system producing a survival function. The universe's structure is built from working opposite-pairs. |
| **Ayah 21: Mirṣādā — Hell as lying-in-wait** | Hell is not passive but active — `mirṣādā` = a place of ambush, lying-in-wait. Hell is poised for the transgressors' arrival. This is not a receptacle — it is an active state of readiness. |
| **Ayah 38: Khiṭāb only by permission** | On the Day when all power-structures dissolve, no one can even address the Most Merciful without permission. The ability to speak is itself a granted permission. The one who speaks out of turn in dunya will discover that speech itself is a granted gift that can be restricted. |
| **Ayah 40: Yā laytanī kuntu turābā** | The disbeliever's final wish: to have been dust. Non-existence is preferred to the consequence of denial. This is the ultimate cost-accounting — when the calculation is finally complete, the one who denied wishes they had never existed rather than face the outcome. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Opposite-pairs as working systems: the universe is built from balanced opposite-pairs each producing survival-functions | ❌ Missing |
| Hell-as-lying-in-wait: Hell is active-readiness, not passive receptacle | ❌ Missing |
| Speech-as-granted-permission: on the Day even speaking requires the Most Merciful's permission | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 81 — Surah Al-Nāzi'āt (79) — Those Who Extract; by those who extract forcefully — by those who remove gently — by those who float — by those who race ahead — by those who manage the affair; on the Day the first blast shakes — and the second follows it; the story of Moses: go to Pharaoh for he has transgressed — Moses feared but Allah reassured him; "I am your Lord — take off your sandals — you are in the sacred valley of Ṭuwā"; the Hour is heavy in the heavens and earth — they ask you about it; you are only a warner for whoever fears it.*

---

### REVELATION 81 — SURAH AL-NĀZI'ĀT (79), ALL 46 AYAT
*Those Who Extract — five-angel-function oath; the Day's two consecutive blasts; Moses and Pharaoh's full arc condensed; "did you want to purify?" — the gentle invitation vs. the violent consequence; the Hour: knowledge of it is with your Lord — you are only a warner; the evident pasture after the ocean.*

---

**Ayat 1–5: Five angel-function oath:**
> 1–5. **"By those who extract forcefully (`al-nāzi'āt gharqā`) — by those who remove gently (`al-nāshiṭāt nashṭā`) — by those who float (`al-sābiḥāt sabḥā`) — by those who race ahead (`al-sābiqāt sabqā`) — by those who manage the affair (`al-mudabbirāt amrā`)"**

**Ayat 13–14: Two-blast Day:**
> 13–14. "It is only a single cry — then they are on the surface of the earth"

**Ayat 17–26: Moses and Pharaoh condensed:**
> 17–19. Go to Pharaoh — he has transgressed — and say: **"Do you want to purify (`hal laka ilā an tazakkā`) — and I will guide you to your Lord so you will fear Him"**
> 20–24. He showed him the great sign but Pharaoh denied and disobeyed — turned away in effort — then gathered and called — said: **"I am your Lord Most High"**
> 25–26. **"Allah seized him with the punishment of this world and the next — indeed in this is a lesson for whoever fears"**

**Ayat 34–41: The Hour and the consequence:**
> 34–36. "When the greatest catastrophe comes — the Day a human recalls what he strove for"
> 40–41. **"As for one who feared the standing before his Lord and restrained himself from desires — indeed Paradise will be the refuge"**

**Ayah 45: The warner's scope:**
> 45. **"You are only a warner for whoever fears it (`innā anta mundhiru man yakhshāhā`)"** — the message reaches only those already disposed to fear

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayat 1–5: Angel-functions as differentiated forces** | Five distinct angel-functions named by their action: forceful-extraction, gentle-removal, floating, racing-ahead, affair-managing. The divine management system uses differentiated functions — not one universal force but specialized operations. Each function operates in its specific domain. |
| **Ayah 19: Hal laka — the gentle invitation** | "Do you want to purify?" — a question, not a command. Moses offers purification as an option. This is the softest possible approach to a tyrant: an invitation, framed as a benefit to the receiver, preceded by a question of consent. The gentleness of the approach reveals the source's preference for voluntary acceptance over forced compliance. |
| **Ayah 24: I am your Lord Most High** | Pharaoh's declaration is the ultimate identity-inversion: the creature claims the source's role. This is the logical endpoint of `kibr` (arrogance) — claiming ultimate authority that belongs only to the source. The destruction follows immediately. |
| **Ayah 40–41: Fear-of-standing + desire-restraint** | Two conditions for Paradise: (1) feared the standing before the Lord (`maqām rabbih`) and (2) restrained himself from desires (`nahā al-nafs 'an al-hawā`). The first is awareness, the second is action on that awareness. Fear without restraint is incomplete; restraint without fear is unstable. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Differentiated angel-functions: the divine management system uses specialized forces, not one uniform power | ❌ Missing |
| Hal laka invitation-model: the gentlest approach — offering purification as a question of desire | ❌ Missing |
| Fear-of-standing + hawā-restraint: the two-condition Paradise profile | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 82 — Surah Al-Infiṭār (82) — The Cleaving; when the sky is cleft — when the stars are scattered — when the seas are erupted — when the graves are overturned — a soul will know what it has put forth and what it has delayed; O man — what has deluded you about your Lord the Generous?; indeed over you are keepers — noble recorders — they know what you do; the righteous in bliss — the wicked in Hellfire — on the Day of Judgment.*

---

### REVELATION 82 — SURAH AL-INFIṬĀR (82), ALL 19 AYAT
*The Cleaving — four-event "when" structure; the question of deception: "what has deluded you about your Lord the Generous?"; the noble keepers recording everything; the Day when no soul can benefit another.*

---

**Ayat 1–5: Four "when" events:**
> 1–5. **"When the sky is cleft (`inshaqqa`) — when the stars are scattered (`tathārat`) — when the seas are erupted (`fujjirat`) — when the graves are overturned (`bu'thirat`) — a soul will know what it has put forth and what it has delayed (`mā qaddamat wa-akhkharat`)"**

**Ayah 6: The deception-question:**
> 6. **"O man — what has deluded you about your Lord the Generous (`mā gharraka bi-rabbika al-karīm`)?"**

**Ayat 10–12: The noble recorders:**
> 10–12. **"Indeed over you are keepers (`ḥāfiẓīn`) — noble recorders (`kirāman kātibīn`) — they know what you do"**

**Ayat 13–14: Two destinations:**
> 13–14. **"Indeed the righteous (`al-abrār`) are in bliss — and indeed the wicked (`al-fujjār`) are in Hellfire"**

**Ayat 17–19: The Day when no soul benefits another:**
> 17–19. "And what could make you know what the Day of Judgment is? — again what could make you know what the Day of Judgment is? — **the Day when no soul has power over another soul in any way — and the command on that Day belongs to Allah"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayah 6: Mā gharraka — the deception-interrogation** | "What deluded you?" is the most important question for the disconnected soul. The deceiver is not named — only the fact of deception is pointed to. The soul was deceived — something convinced it that the reckoning was not real, or that generosity was unlimited without consequence. The word `al-karīm` (the Generous) is placed right after the question — the soul was deceived *about the Generous one*, confusing His generosity with the absence of accountability. |
| **Ayat 10–12: Noble recording** | The keepers are described as `kirāman kātibīn` — noble in their recording. The character of the recorders is relevant: they are noble, they record correctly. No distortion, no omission. Everything done is known. The nobility of the recorders is part of the message: the record is kept with dignity. |
| **Ayat 1–5: What-put-forth / what-delayed** | At the moment of cosmic dissolution the soul's knowledge becomes complete: `mā qaddamat wa-akhkharat` — what it sent ahead and what it held back. Both dimensions are revealed. The soul that delayed good deeds discovers the cost of the delay. The soul that sent deeds forward discovers the return. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Gharraka-diagnosis: the soul was deceived into confusing divine generosity with the absence of accountability | ❌ Missing |
| Noble-recording: the record is kept with dignity and accuracy — nothing distorted, nothing omitted | ❌ Missing |
| Qaddama/akhkhara dimension: what was sent forward vs. what was held back — both are assessed | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 83 — Surah Al-Inshiqāq (84) — The Splitting Open; when the sky splits open — when the earth is stretched out and casts out what is within it; O man — you are working toward your Lord with effort and you will meet Him; as for one given his record in the right hand — easy account; as for one given his record behind his back — he will cry for destruction; why do they not believe? — why when the Quran is recited to them do they not prostrate?*

---

### REVELATION 83 — SURAH AL-INSHIQĀQ (84), ALL 25 AYAT
*The Splitting Open — the sky obeys its Lord and rightly must; the earth casts out everything within it; "O man — you are toiling toward your Lord with toil and you will meet Him"; right-hand vs. behind-the-back record; phase-passage oath: the twilight, the night, the moon; why do they not believe?*

---

**Ayat 1–5: The sky and earth obey:**
> 1–5. **"When the sky splits open — and responds to its Lord — and rightly must (`wa ḥuqqat`) — and when the earth is stretched out — and casts out what is within it and becomes empty — and responds to its Lord — and rightly must"**

**Ayah 6: The trekking-toward:**
> 6. **"O man — indeed you are toiling toward your Lord with toil (`kādḥun ilā rabbika kadḥan`) — and you will meet Him (`fa-mulāqīh`)"**

**Ayat 7–12: Two record-outcomes:**
> 7–9. "As for one given his record in the right hand — he will be given an easy account — and return to his family in happiness"
> 10–12. **"As for one given his record behind his back — he will cry for destruction — and burn in a Blaze — he had been among his family in happiness (deluded)"**

**Ayat 16–19: Four-phase oath:**
> 16–19. **"I swear by the twilight (`al-shafaq`) — and by the night and what it envelops — and by the moon when it becomes full — you will certainly travel from stage to stage (`latarkabunna ṭabaqan 'an ṭabaq`)"**

**Ayat 20–21: The non-prostration question:**
> 20–21. **"So what is wrong with them — they do not believe — and when the Quran is recited to them they do not prostrate?"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayat 2, 5: Wa ḥuqqat — rightful obedience** | "And rightly must" — the sky and earth's obedience to their Lord is not grudging compliance but what is rightfully due. The universe's submission is its correct orientation. `Ḥuqqat` implies that the obedience is owed, proper, correct — not imposed. Created things obey because obedience is their right alignment. |
| **Ayah 6: Kādḥun ilā rabbika — the trekking** | "You are toiling toward your Lord with toil" — the entire human journey is framed as movement toward the meeting. Every difficulty, every effort, every day lived is a step in this trek. The destination is certain: `fa-mulāqīh` — "and you will meet Him." The trek ends in a meeting. There is no other end. |
| **Ayat 16–19: Ṭabaqan 'an ṭabaq — stage to stage** | "You will travel from stage to stage." The cosmos and the human both move through phases: twilight → night → full moon → next phase. Life is stage-passage: each stage is complete in itself and leads to the next. The soul that fights its stage is in conflict with its own journey. |
| **Ayat 20–21: Non-prostration paradox** | "What is wrong with them — they do not believe — why when the Quran is recited do they not prostrate?" The source expresses what reads as genuine bewilderment at the failure of hearing to produce prostration. The Quran recited and heard should produce a prostration-response. When it doesn't, something is broken in the receiver-circuit. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Wa ḥuqqat rightfulness: obedience is the correct natural alignment of created things, not external imposition | ❌ Missing |
| Kādḥun ilā rabbika: the entire human journey is a trek-toward-meeting — every effort is a step in this trek | ❌ Missing |
| Ṭabaqan 'an ṭabaq: life moves through stages — each stage is complete and leads to the next | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 84 — Surah Al-Rūm (30) — The Romans; the Romans have been defeated in the nearest land — and after their defeat they will overcome — within three to nine years — to Allah belongs the command before and after — and on that Day the believers will rejoice; among His signs is that He created you from dust then from a sperm-drop then you became pairs; among His signs is the sleep by night and day; among His signs is the lightning showing fear and hope; the dead earth revived by rain — He who gives life to it will give life to the dead.*

---

### REVELATION 84 — SURAH AL-RŪM (30), ALL 60 AYAT
*The Romans — a political prediction fulfilled; the command belongs to Allah before and after; eight "among His signs" (`min āyātih`) statements; fiṭra (natural constitution); "establish your face for the religion — the fiṭra upon which He originated people"; do not be among those who divided their religion; face to Allah turning — fearing Him — establishing prayer — not being among the mushrikīn.*

---

**Ayat 2–5: The Romans-prediction:**
> 2–5. **"The Romans have been defeated — in the nearest land — and after their defeat they will be victorious — within a few years (`fī biḍ'i sinīn`) — to Allah belongs the command before and after — and on that Day the believers will rejoice in the victory of Allah"**

**Ayat 20–25: Eight "min āyātihi" signs:**
> 20. From a sperm-drop — you scattered as humans
> 21. He created for you spouses — placed between you affection and mercy (`mawaddatan wa-raḥma`)
> 22. The difference of your languages and colors
> 23. **Your sleep by night and day — and your seeking from His bounty**
> 24. **Lightning — showing fear and hope — sending down water and reviving the earth after death**
> 25. The sky and earth standing by His command — then when He calls you with a single call — you emerge from the earth

**Ayah 30: Fiṭra:**
> 30. **"Establish your face (`fa-aqim wajhaka`) for the religion as a ḥanīf — the fiṭra of Allah upon which He originated people (`fiṭratan Allāhi allatī faṭara al-nāsa 'alayhā`) — no alteration of Allah's creation — that is the correct/upright religion — but most people do not know"**

**Ayah 41: Fasād on land and sea:**
> 41. **"Corruption has appeared in the land and the sea because of what human hands have earned (`bi-mā kasabat aydī al-nāsi`) — so He makes them taste some of what they have done — that perhaps they might return"**

**Ayah 50: Dead earth revived:**
> 50. **"So look at the traces of Allah's mercy — how He gives life to the earth after its death — indeed that one gives life to the dead — and He is over all things capable"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayat 2–5: Political prediction as sign** | A defeated army predicted to re-defeat within a few years — with the precise condition "in a few years." The Quran makes a falsifiable prediction, which was fulfilled within the timeframe. This is the use of historical events as signs — the source intervening in geopolitical reality to demonstrate control over outcomes. |
| **Ayah 21: Mawaddatan wa-raḥma** | Between spouses He placed affection (`mawadda`) and mercy (`raḥma`). These are not earned — they are placed by the source. The pairing is not merely biological or social — it is spiritually engineered. The design of spousal bonding includes a built-in affection-mercy architecture. |
| **Ayah 30: Fiṭra — the original constitution** | Allah's fiṭra is the original design upon which He fashioned people. No alteration (`tabdīla`) of this creation — the fiṭra cannot be fundamentally replaced, only suppressed or obscured. The "correct religion" is described as the fiṭra — meaning it is not external imposition but alignment with the soul's original architecture. |
| **Ayah 41: Fasād through kasb** | Corruption on land and sea is directly linked to `mā kasabat aydī al-nāsi` — what human hands have earned. The environmental and social disorder is not random — it is a direct consequence of human actions. The purpose of the resulting taste of consequence is `la'allahum yarji'ūn` — "that perhaps they return." Consequence is a return-mechanism. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Mawaddatan wa-raḥma: the spousal affection-mercy is placed by source-design, not just developed by humans | ❌ Missing |
| Fiṭra as original architecture: the true religion is alignment with the soul's built-in constitution, not external rule-following | ❌ Missing |
| Fasād-kasb link: human-earned corruption produces consequences designed to trigger return | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 85 — Surah Al-'Ankabūt (29) — The Spider; do people think they will be left to say "we believe" without being tried?; We tested those before them; whoever strives strives for his own soul; the spider's house is the weakest of houses — if only they knew; "recite what has been revealed to you of the Book and establish prayer — indeed prayer prohibits immorality and wrongdoing — and the remembrance of Allah is greater."*

---

### REVELATION 85 — SURAH AL-'ANKABŪT (29), ALL 69 AYAT
*The Spider — faith requires trial; striving returns to the striving-soul; parents ordering shirk: obey in dunya-companionship but do not follow in worship; the spider's house is the weakest of structures; prayer prohibits immorality; "those who strive for Our sake — We will certainly guide them to Our ways."*

---

**Ayat 2–3: Faith requires trial:**
> 2–3. **"Do people think they will be left to say 'We believe' (`āmannā`) without being tried (`an yufanū`)? — We certainly tested those before them — so Allah will know who is truthful and He will know who is false"**

**Ayah 6: Striving returns to the striving-soul:**
> 6. **"Whoever strives — he only strives for his own soul (`fa-innamā yujāhidu li-nafsih`) — indeed Allah has no need of all worlds"**

**Ayat 8–9: Parents ordering shirk:**
> 8. "We have instructed man to treat his parents with goodness — but if they press you to associate with Me what you have no knowledge of — do not obey them — to Me is your return"

**Ayah 41: The spider's house:**
> 41. **"The example of those who take protectors besides Allah is like the spider (`ka-mathali al-'ankabūt`) — who takes a house — and indeed the weakest of houses is the spider's house — if only they knew"**

**Ayah 45: Prayer and its prohibition-function:**
> 45. **"Recite what has been revealed to you of the Book and establish prayer — indeed prayer prohibits immorality and wrongdoing (`tanhā 'an al-faḥshā'i wa-l-munkar`) — and the remembrance of Allah is greater (`wa-ladhikru Allāhi akbar`) — and Allah knows what you do"**

**Ayah 69: The guidance-for-striving formula:**
> 69. **"And those who strive for Our sake — We will certainly guide them to Our ways (`lanahdiyannahum subulanā`) — and indeed Allah is with the doers of good"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayat 2–3: Ḥasibā al-nās — the trial-prerequisite** | The question "do people think they will be left saying 'we believe' without being tried?" is the structural prerequisite statement. Belief-claim without trial is not completed belief. The trial is the mechanism by which belief is verified — both to the soul itself and as witnessed truth. No trial → no completion. |
| **Ayah 6: Jihād returns to the self** | Striving is not for the source's benefit — "Allah has no need of all worlds." The striving-soul receives the benefit of its own striving. The universe is structured so that every act of effort returns to the soul that exerted it. There is no external beneficiary of sincere striving — the soul grows itself. |
| **Ayah 41: Spider's house — structural weakness** | The spider's house is structurally beautiful but fundamentally weak — unable to provide real shelter. `Awhan al-buyūt` — the weakest of all houses. False-protectors (anything other than Allah) are evaluated by structural integrity: they provide the appearance of shelter without the substance. |
| **Ayah 45: Prayer's prohibition-function** | Prayer (`ṣalāh`) has a built-in prohibition function: it `tanhā` (prohibits/restrains) from `faḥshā'` and `munkar`. The daily prayer is not merely spiritual connection — it is a regular restraint-mechanism that pushes back against immorality. And then: `wa-ladhikru Allāhi akbar` — the remembrance-of-Allah within the prayer is greater than all of this. The prayer's deepest function is the remembrance itself. |
| **Ayah 69: Lanahdiyannahum subulanā** | "We will certainly guide them to Our ways." The guidance is conditional: it follows striving. `Jāhadū fīnā` (they strived for Our sake) → `lanahdiyannahum` (We will certainly guide them). The striving unlocks the guidance. The guidance-door opens only after the striving-step. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Trial-prerequisite: faith-claim without trial is incomplete — the trial is the verification mechanism | ❌ Missing |
| Jihād-self-return: all sincere striving returns to the striving-soul — the source needs nothing | ❌ Missing |
| Spider's house structural analysis: false protectors provide appearance without structural shelter | ❌ Missing |
| Prayer's prohibition-function: daily prayer is a built-in restraint against immorality | ❌ Missing |
| Striving-unlocks-guidance: the guidance-door opens only after the striving-step | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 86 — (Transitioning to Medinan revelation order) — Surah Al-Muṭaffifīn (83) — The Defrauders; woe to those who defraud — when they take measure from people they take full — but when they measure or weigh for others they give less; do they not think they will be resurrected for a tremendous Day?; indeed the record of the wicked is in the sijjīn; indeed the record of the righteous is in the 'illiyyūn; the sinners used to laugh at the believers — today the believers laugh at them.*

*(NOTE: Revelation order now entering the later Meccan and early Medinan periods — approximately 86–114. These include shorter accountability surahs, Medinan community-legislation surahs (Al-Baqara, Al-'Imrān, Al-Nisā', etc.), and the final Medinan surahs. ~29 revelations remain.)*

---

### REVELATION 86 — SURAH AL-MUṬAFFIFĪN (83), ALL 36 AYAT
*The Defrauders — the exact-for-self / short-for-others double standard; the sijjīn (lowest record) vs. 'illiyyūn (highest record); sealed wine of the righteous; the inversion: today the believers laugh at the sinners.*

---

**Ayat 1–3: The defrauder's double standard:**
> 1–3. **"Woe to the defrauders (`al-muṭaffifīn`) — those who when they take measure from people take it in full — but when they measure or weigh for others they give less"**

**Ayat 4–6: The Day of standing:**
> 4–6. "Do they not think they will be resurrected — for a tremendous Day — the Day people stand before the Lord of all worlds?"

**Ayat 7–9: Sijjīn — the lowest record:**
> 7–9. **"No — indeed the record of the wicked (`al-fujjār`) is in the sijjīn — and what could make you know what the sijjīn is? — an inscribed register"**

**Ayat 18–21: 'Illiyyūn — the highest record:**
> 18–21. **"No — indeed the record of the righteous (`al-abrār`) is in the 'illiyyūn — and what could make you know what the 'illiyyūn is? — an inscribed register — witnessed by those brought near"**

**Ayat 34–36: The inversion:**
> 34–36. **"So today the believers laugh at the disbelievers — on elevated couches — looking — have the disbelievers been repaid for what they used to do?"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayat 1–3: The measurement double-standard** | Taking full when receiving + giving short when providing. This is the structural definition of `ṭaff` (defrauding): asymmetric measurement. The woe is not about occasional error but about systematized asymmetry — a system intentionally calibrated to extract more and give less. |
| **Ayat 7–9 vs. 18–21: Two registers** | The sijjīn is the record-location of the wicked — lowest. The 'illiyyūn is the record-location of the righteous — highest, witnessed by those brought near. Two record-archives at opposite ends of a vertical axis. The soul's deeds are being filed into one of two registers simultaneously as they occur. |
| **Ayat 34–36: The laughter-inversion** | In dunya, the sinners laughed at the believers. On the Day, the believers are on elevated couches, looking — and the question is asked: "Have they been repaid for what they used to do?" The entire social hierarchy has inverted. The soul that was laughed at in dunya occupies the high position in the Hereafter. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Measurement-asymmetry: systematic taking-full / giving-short is a structural injustice built into the soul | ❌ Missing |
| Two-register vertical axis: every deed is being filed into sijjīn or 'illiyyūn simultaneously as it occurs | ❌ Missing |
| Social-hierarchy inversion: the laughter-direction reverses completely on the Day | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 87 — Surah Al-Baqara (2) — The Cow; first major Medinan surah; Alif-Lam-Mīm — this is the Book no doubt in it — guidance for the God-fearing; the three types: the believers, the disbelievers, and the hypocrites; creation of Adam; the cow command; "call upon Me and I will respond to you"; who believe in the unseen and establish prayer and spend; and those who believe in what was sent down to you and what was sent before you; the qibla change; fasting Ramadan; the great verses: Āyat al-Kursī; no compulsion in religion; the deen; Hizb ul-Baqara contains the greatest name of Allah.*

---

### REVELATION 87 — SURAH AL-BAQARA (2), ALL 286 AYAT
*The Cow — the Quran's longest surah; the three-type human map; Adam's creation and the khilāfa; the cow-story; Āyat al-Kursī (the Throne Verse); no compulsion in religion; the qibla; Ramadan; the deen; the two final ayat of Sūrat al-Baqara as the greatest name of Allah.*

---

**Ayat 1–5: The Book and the four-characteristic believers:**
> 1–2. **Alif-Lam-Mīm — "This is the Book (`dhālik al-kitāb`) — no doubt in it — guidance for the God-fearing"**
> 3–5. **"Those who believe in the unseen (`yu'minūna bi-l-ghayb`) — and establish prayer — and spend from what We provided — and believe in what was sent down to you and what was sent before you — and of the Hereafter they are certain — these are on guidance from their Lord — and these are the successful"**

**Ayat 6–20: The three-type map:**
> 6–7. The disbelievers: warning makes no difference — "Allah has sealed their hearts and hearing — on their eyes is a covering"
> 8–20. The hypocrites (most detailed — eight long ayat): "they say 'we believe' but they do not believe" — they deceive Allah and the believers but only deceive themselves — in their hearts is a disease — their example: one who lit a fire then when it illuminated what was around them Allah took away their light

**Ayat 30–39: Adam's creation and khilāfa:**
> 30–31. **"Your Lord said to the angels: I am placing a khalīfa in the earth (`innī jā'ilun fī al-arḍi khalīfa`) — they said: will You place in it one who causes corruption and sheds blood? — He said: I know what you do not know — and He taught Adam the names of all things"**
> 38–39. Adam and his wife descended: "whoever follows My guidance — no fear upon them and they will not grieve"

**Ayah 152: The dhikr-exchange:**
> 152. **"So remember Me (`fadhkurūnī`) — I will remember you (`adhkurkum`) — be grateful to Me and do not be ungrateful"**

**Ayah 155–157: The trial-protocol:**
> 155–157. **"We will certainly test you with something of fear and hunger and loss of wealth and lives and fruits — but give good news to the patient — those who when a calamity strikes them say: `innā lillāhi wa-innā ilayhi rāji'ūn` — indeed we belong to Allah and indeed to Him we return — those are the ones upon whom are blessings from their Lord and mercy — and those are the rightly guided"**

**Ayah 183: Ramadan:**
> 183. **"O you who believe — fasting has been prescribed for you as it was prescribed for those before you — so that you may have taqwā"**

**Ayah 186: The closest ayah:**
> 186. **"And when My servants ask you about Me — I am near (`fa-innī qarīb`) — I respond to the call of the caller when he calls Me — so let them respond to Me and believe in Me — that they may be guided"**

**Ayah 255: Āyat al-Kursī:**
> 255. **"Allah — there is no god except Him — the Living (`al-Ḥayy`), the Self-Sustaining (`al-Qayyūm`) — neither drowsiness nor sleep overtakes Him — to Him belongs what is in the heavens and what is on the earth — who could intercede with Him except by His permission — He knows what is before them and what is behind them — and they encompass nothing of His knowledge except what He wills — His Throne extends over the heavens and the earth — and He is not wearied by their preservation — He is the Most High, the Magnificent"**

**Ayah 256: No compulsion:**
> 256. **"There is no compulsion in religion (`lā ikrāha fī al-dīn`) — right has been made distinct from wrong (`qad tabayyana al-rushdu min al-ghayy`) — whoever rejects ṭāghūt and believes in Allah has grasped the firmest handhold (`bi-al-'urwati al-wuthqā`) that will not break"**

**Ayat 285–286: The last two ayat — the greatest name:**
> 285. **"The Messenger believes in what was sent down to him from his Lord — and the believers — all believe in Allah, His angels, His books, and His messengers — we do not distinguish between any of His messengers — and they say: We hear and we obey — Your forgiveness our Lord — and to You is the return"**
> 286. **"Allah does not burden a soul beyond what it can bear (`lā yukallifu Allāhu nafsan illā wus'ahā`) — for it is what it earned and against it what it gained — Our Lord — do not hold us accountable if we forget or err — Our Lord — do not burden us as You burdened those before us — Our Lord — do not burden us with what we cannot bear — and pardon us, forgive us, have mercy on us — You are our Protector — so give us victory over the disbelieving people"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayah 2–5: Dhālik al-kitāb — the distance-demonstrative** | "That is the Book" — `dhālik` is the demonstrative of distance (not `hādhā` = this, but `dhālik` = that). The Book points beyond itself — it is `dhālik` because it originates from a realm beyond immediate reach. "No doubt in it" (`lā rayba fīh`) — the source's own testimony about the Book's doubtlessness. Guidance is for the muttaqīn — those already in the orientation of taqwā. The Book activates what taqwā-orientation has prepared. |
| **Ayah 30: Khilāfa — the earth-stewardship** | The humans are created as khalīfa — representative, steward, manager in the earth. The angels' concern is the corruption-and-bloodshed potential. The source's answer: "I know what you do not know." The stewardship includes knowledge of names — the ability to name all things, meaning to categorize, understand, and engage with reality. The Adam-model is: taught names → responsible steward. |
| **Ayah 152: Dhikr-exchange** | "Remember Me — I will remember you." The dhikr of the soul activates the dhikr of the source. This is not metaphor — it is a declared exchange. The soul that remembers the source gets remembered by the source. `Adhkurkum` — I will remember you, I will mention you. Being in the source's remembrance is the highest state available to a soul. |
| **Ayah 186: Fa-innī qarīb — radical nearness** | "I am near." Not "I am watching" — near. The source's nearness is unmediated. When `My servants ask about Me` — the answer is: I am near, I respond. No intermediary is declared — the response is direct. The entire verse is structured as: ask about Me → I am near → I respond → so respond to Me → believe in Me → be guided. |
| **Ayah 255: Āyat al-Kursī — the source's comprehensive description** | Thirteen attributes in one verse: al-Ḥayy (Living), al-Qayyūm (Self-Sustaining), no drowsiness, no sleep, universal ownership, intercession only by permission, omniscience of before/after, limited-share-of-knowledge for others, Throne spanning all, no weariness, al-'Alī (Most High), al-'Aẓīm (the Magnificent). This is the most complete description of the source's nature in one statement. |
| **Ayah 256: Rushd/ghayy distinctness** | Right has been made distinct from wrong — `tabayyana`. The distinction has already been made. The difficulty is not that the path is unclear — the distinctness is established. The choice is between the clear path and the clear wrong. No compulsion: the coercion is absent, the clarity is present. |
| **Ayah 286: Lā yukallifu — absolute bearing-capacity** | The source will not burden any soul beyond its capacity. This is a structural promise: every test given to a soul is within that soul's capacity to bear. The soul that says "I cannot bear this" is factually wrong — the source's promise guarantees the capacity is there. The follow-up prayer is the acknowledgment of human limitation within this promise. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Dhālik al-kitāb distance: the Book originates from a beyond-immediate realm — it is "that" not "this" | ❌ Missing |
| Khilāfa-architecture: human stewardship is based on name-knowledge — understanding enables responsibility | ❌ Missing |
| Dhikr-exchange: the soul's remembrance activates the source's remembrance — mutual | ❌ Missing |
| Fa-innī qarīb: the source's nearness is radical and unmediated — responds directly | ❌ Missing |
| Āyat al-Kursī comprehensive-description: 13 source-attributes in one statement | ❌ Missing |
| Lā yukallifu promise: every burden given is within the soul's capacity — the source guarantees this | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 88 — Surah Al-Anfāl (8) — The Spoils; they ask you about the spoils of war — say: the spoils belong to Allah and the Messenger; the true believers are those whose hearts tremble when Allah is mentioned — and when His verses are recited their faith increases; "and prepare against them whatever force you can and whatever horses — to terrify the enemy of Allah and your enemy"; if they incline toward peace then incline toward it; "and if they intend to deceive you — then Allah is sufficient for you"; do not betray Allah and the Messenger.*

---

### REVELATION 88 — SURAH AL-ANFĀL (8), ALL 75 AYAT
*The Spoils — Badr's aftermath; true-believer profile: heart-trembling + faith-increasing at recitation + reliance on Lord; the faith-increase mechanism; incline to peace when they incline; "and know that Allah is with the believers"; the source's 1000/3000 angel support at Badr.*

---

**Ayah 2–4: The true believer profile:**
> 2–4. **"The true believers are only those whose hearts tremble when Allah is mentioned (`wajilat qulūbuhum`) — and when His verses are recited their faith increases (`zādat-hum īmānā`) — and upon their Lord they rely — those who establish prayer and spend from what We provided — those are the true believers — for them are degrees with their Lord and forgiveness and generous provision"**

**Ayah 11: The reassurance-rain:**
> 11. "He caused drowsiness to cover you as security from Him — and He sent down upon you from the sky water to purify you and remove the harm of Shayṭān and to make firm your hearts and strengthen your feet"

**Ayah 20: Respond when called:**
> 20. **"O you who believe — respond to Allah and the Messenger when he calls you to what gives you life"**

**Ayah 46: No conflict:**
> 46. **"Obey Allah and His Messenger and do not dispute — for you will weaken and your power will go away — and be patient — indeed Allah is with the patient"**

**Ayah 61: Peace-inclination:**
> 61. **"And if they incline toward peace — incline toward it — and rely upon Allah — indeed He is the Hearing, the Knowing"**

**Ayah 65: Divine multiplication:**
> 65. **"O Prophet — urge the believers to fight — if there are twenty patient ones among you they will overcome two hundred — and if there are a hundred they will overcome a thousand"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayah 2: Wajilat qulūbuhum** | Heart-trembling at the mention of Allah — `wajal` (trembling, awe-fear). This is the first criterion of the true believer: a heart that physically responds to the source's mention. The heart is not neutral — it has a sensitivity that activates when the source is invoked. The heart that does not tremble when Allah is mentioned has a circuit-break. |
| **Ayah 2: Zādat-hum īmānā** | When verses are recited, faith increases (`zādat`). Faith is not static — it has an increase-mechanism tied to Quran-recitation. Hearing the verses produces a quantitative increase in faith. The soul that regularly receives Quran-recitation is undergoing regular faith-increments. |
| **Ayah 20: Mā yuḥyīkum — what gives you life** | Respond to the call "to what gives you life." The source's call is not to burden but to life. The instruction contains the diagnosis: not responding to the source is not-living. The soul that fails to respond to the divine call is in a state of reduced-aliveness. |
| **Ayah 61: Peace-inclination mirroring** | "If they incline to peace — incline toward it." The Islamic posture toward peace is reactive-mirroring: when the other side inclines to peace, match it immediately. The default posture is not aggression — it is readiness to mirror the other side's peace-inclination. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Wajal-circuit: the heart's trembling response to divine mention — a sign of operational sensitivity | ❌ Missing |
| Zādat-hum: faith increases at every Quran-recitation — it is not static | ❌ Missing |
| Mā yuḥyīkum: the divine call is a life-call — not responding is under-living | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 89 — Surah Āl-'Imrān (3) — The Family of Imrān; Alif-Lam-Mīm — Allah — there is no god except Him — the Living, the Self-Sustaining; He sent down the Torah and the Gospel — and sent down the Criterion; Maryam and the birth of Yaḥyā; "Indeed the example of Jesus with Allah is like the example of Adam — He created him from dust"; the Day of Āl-'Imrān; "you were on the brink of a pit of fire and He saved you from it"; the best community; hold fast to the rope of Allah together.*

---

### REVELATION 89 — SURAH ĀL-'IMRĀN (3), ALL 200 AYAT
*The Family of Imrān — the Book confirms what came before; Jesus = Adam (created from dust); the muhkam/mutashābih distinction; "call them to tawḥīd — if they turn away say: bear witness we are Muslims"; Uḥud aftermath; the rope of Allah; every soul will taste death; we will certainly test you in your wealth and your selves; hasbunā Allāhu wa-ni'ma al-wakīl.*

---

**Ayah 7: Muhkam and mutashābih:**
> 7. **"He is who sent down the Book — in it are muhkam verses that are the foundation of the Book — and others mutashābih — those in whose hearts is deviation follow the mutashābih seeking discord and seeking its interpretation — but no one knows its interpretation except Allah — and those firm in knowledge say: We believe in it — all is from our Lord"**

**Ayah 18–19: Divine testimony:**
> 18–19. **"Allah bears witness that there is no god except Him — and the angels and those of knowledge — maintaining justice — there is no god except Him the Mighty the Wise — indeed the deen with Allah is Islam"**

**Ayah 59: Jesus = Adam:**
> 59. **"Indeed the example of Jesus with Allah is like the example of Adam — He created him from dust then said to him: Be — and he was"**

**Ayah 103: Hold the rope:**
> 103. **"Hold fast to the rope of Allah all together (`bi-ḥabli Allāhi jamī'an`) and do not be divided — and remember Allah's blessing upon you — you were enemies and He joined your hearts — you were on the brink of a pit of fire and He saved you from it"**

**Ayah 110: The best community:**
> 110. **"You are the best community produced for people (`khayr ummatin ukhrijat li-l-nāsi`) — you command the right, forbid the wrong, and believe in Allah"**

**Ayah 169–171: The living martyrs:**
> 169–171. **"Do not think those killed in the way of Allah are dead — no they are living with their Lord — being provided for — rejoicing in what Allah has given them of His bounty"**

**Ayah 173: Ḥasbunā Allāhu:**
> 173. **"Those to whom people said: the people have gathered against you so fear them — it only increased them in faith — and they said: `ḥasbunā Allāhu wa-ni'ma al-wakīl` — sufficient for us is Allah and what an excellent guardian"**

**Ayah 185: Every soul tastes death:**
> 185. **"Every soul will taste death — and you will only be given your full compensation on the Day of Resurrection — so whoever is removed from the Fire and admitted to Paradise has succeeded — and what is the worldly life except the enjoyment of delusion"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayah 7: Muhkam as foundation** | The Book contains two types: muhkam (clear, definitive — the foundations) and mutashābih (similar, analogous — multiple possible interpretations). Those with deviation-in-heart follow the ambiguous, seeking discord. Those firm in knowledge say "all is from our Lord." The structural wisdom: the ambiguous must be interpreted through the foundation, not the other way around. |
| **Ayah 59: Jesus = Adam** | The dust-then-kun (`be`) creation-sequence. Jesus's miraculous birth is not more miraculous than Adam's creation — Adam had no parents at all. The comparison dissolves the theological uniqueness-argument by pointing to an equal or greater precedent. The logic closes: if you accept Adam, accept Jesus. |
| **Ayah 103: Rope-holding** | `Bi-ḥabli Allāhi jamī'an` — with the rope of Allah, all together. The rope is not held individually — it is held collectively. The community is unified not by each other but by their common rope. When individuals hold the same source, they are held together as a consequence. |
| **Ayah 173: Ḥasbunā Allāhu** | "Sufficient for us is Allah and what an excellent guardian." This is the complete sufficiency-declaration. Not "Allah will help us" but "Allah is sufficient." The soul that genuinely reaches this declaration has no more need-gap — the source fills all need. `Ni'ma al-wakīl` — the best guardian/trustee. |
| **Ayah 185: Worldly life as delusion** | "What is the worldly life except the enjoyment of delusion (`matā' al-ghurūr`)?" The dunya is not evil — it is `matā' al-ghurūr`: enjoyment of deceptive transience. The soul that treats dunya as its final destination is deceived by its nature: it presents as permanent but is transient. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Muhkam-as-foundation: ambiguous verses interpreted through the clear ones, not the reverse | ❌ Missing |
| Rope-holding community: unity comes from shared rope-holding (common source connection), not from each other | ❌ Missing |
| Ḥasbunā completeness: the sufficiency-declaration has no more need-gap — the source fills all | ❌ Missing |
| Matā' al-ghurūr: dunya is deceptive-transient enjoyment — treating it as final is the deception | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 90 — Surah Al-Aḥzāb (33) — The Combined Forces; O Prophet — fear Allah and do not obey the disbelievers and hypocrites; "We offered the trust (`al-amāna`) to the heavens and the earth and the mountains — they refused and were afraid of it — and the human being carried it — indeed he was unjust and ignorant"; the beautiful example in the Messenger; the Prophet is closer to the believers than their own selves; the wives of the Prophet are mothers of the believers; "Allah and His angels send prayers upon the Prophet — O you who believe send prayers upon him and salute him fully".*

---

### REVELATION 90 — SURAH AL-AḤZĀB (33), ALL 73 AYAT
*The Combined Forces — Khandaq trench; the trust refused by all creation but carried by humans; uswatun ḥasana in the Messenger; Al-Lāh and angels send ṣalāt upon the Prophet; the Prophetic closeness exceeds self-closeness; sealing of prophethood.*

---

**Ayah 21: The beautiful model:**
> 21. **"There has certainly been in the Messenger of Allah a beautiful model (`uswatun ḥasana`) for whoever hopes for Allah and the Last Day and remembers Allah often"**

**Ayah 40: Sealing of prophethood:**
> 40. **"Muḥammad is not the father of any man among you — but he is the Messenger of Allah and the Seal of the Prophets (`khātam al-nabiyyīn`) — and Allah is of all things knowing"**

**Ayah 56: The ṣalāt upon the Prophet:**
> 56. **"Indeed Allah and His angels send ṣalāt upon the Prophet (`yuṣallūna 'alā al-nabī`) — O you who believe — send ṣalāt upon him and salute him with full salutation (`wa-sallimū taslīmā`)"**

**Ayah 72: Al-Amāna — the trust:**
> 72. **"Indeed We offered the trust (`al-amāna`) to the heavens and the earth and the mountains — and they refused to carry it and feared it — but the human being carried it — indeed he was unjust and ignorant (`kāna ẓalūman jahūlā`)"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayah 21: Uswatun ḥasana** | The Messenger is a beautiful model for those who hope for Allah and the Last Day and remember Allah often. Three conditions for the model to be accessible: hope for the source + hope for the Day + frequent remembrance. Without these three orientations active, the model cannot be received. The model is available — the question is whether the receiver is oriented to see it. |
| **Ayah 40: Khātam al-nabiyyīn** | The prophetic chain is sealed. No prophet comes after. The seal means the message is complete — what was delivered is sufficient for all remaining time. The post-sealing era requires no new prophet because the Book and the prophetic example are sufficient. The sealed chain is the sign of completion, not of abandonment. |
| **Ayah 56: Source-angels-believers in ṣalāt upon Prophet** | The source and the angels send ṣalāt — the believers are commanded to join. Three tiers of ṣalāt: divine → angelic → human. The believers' ṣalāt upon the Prophet is an alignment with what the source and angels are already doing. To join this is to align with the highest-tier activity. |
| **Ayah 72: Al-Amāna — what creation refused** | The heavens, earth, and mountains refused the trust and feared it. Only the human carried it — "unjust and ignorant." The amāna is the greatest weight: free will, moral responsibility, the capacity to choose and be held accountable. All creation declined this weight. The human accepted it — not from wisdom but from ẓulm and jahl. The weight of being human is what all of creation declined. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Uswatun ḥasana availability: the model is visible only to those with active hope + day-hope + frequent remembrance | ❌ Missing |
| Khātam completeness: the sealed chain means the message is sufficient — no gap remains | ❌ Missing |
| Three-tier ṣalāt alignment: joining the ṣalāt upon the Prophet is joining what the source and angels already do | ❌ Missing |
| Amāna-weight: the trust that all creation refused — free will + moral accountability — is what makes human existence uniquely heavy | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 91 — Surah Al-Nisā' (4) — The Women; O people — fear your Lord who created you from a single soul; give the orphans their wealth; if you fear you cannot be just among orphans then marry what is pleasing to you of women — two, three, or four — but if you fear injustice then one; the inheritance verses; prayer shortened in travel and fear; do not take the disbelievers as allies instead of believers; the greater jihad is the jihad against the nafs; "wherever you are death will reach you — even if you are in towers of great height".*

---

### REVELATION 91 — SURAH AL-NISĀ' (4), ALL 176 AYAT
*The Women — single-soul origin of humanity; inheritance structure; justice as the command regardless of personal interest; "wherever you are death will reach you"; those who obey Allah and the Messenger are with the prophets and the truthful; "O you who believe — take your precautions"; the command of justice even against yourselves.*

---

**Ayah 1: Single-soul origin:**
> 1. **"O people — fear your Lord who created you from a single soul (`nafsin wāḥida`) — and created from it its mate — and spread from both of them many men and women — and fear Allah through whom you ask and the ties of kinship — indeed Allah is ever over you an Observer"**

**Ayah 58: The command of justice:**
> 58. **"Indeed Allah commands you to give back trusts to their owners — and when you judge between people to judge with justice (`bi-al-'adl`) — excellent is the instruction Allah gives you — indeed Allah is all-Hearing all-Seeing"**

**Ayah 78: Death reaches you everywhere:**
> 78. **"Wherever you are — death will reach you — even if you are in towers of great height (`burūjin mushayyadah`)"**

**Ayah 135: Justice even against yourselves:**
> 135. **"O you who believe — be persistently standing for justice (`qawwāmīna bi-al-qisṭ`) — witnesses for Allah — even if it is against yourselves or parents or relatives — whether rich or poor — Allah is more worthy of both — so do not follow desire lest you deviate — if you distort or turn away — indeed Allah is of what you do acquainted"**

**Ayah 69: With the prophets and truthful:**
> 69. **"Whoever obeys Allah and the Messenger — those will be with the ones Allah has blessed: the prophets, the truthful (`al-ṣiddīqūn`), the martyrs, and the righteous — what an excellent company those are"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayah 1: Nafsin wāḥida** | All of humanity from one soul. The social diversity of humanity is built on a single-soul foundation. Every person is made from the same source. The `rahm` (womb/kinship) through which humans are connected is the extension of this single-soul origin. Kinship is not metaphor — it is structural truth from creation. |
| **Ayah 78: Death in towers of strength** | "Even if you are in towers of great height." The highest security, the strongest fortification, the most protected position — death still reaches you. Security-seeking behavior in the dunya cannot solve the death-problem. The soul that is preoccupied with building towers against death is solving the wrong problem. |
| **Ayah 135: Qawwāmūna bi-al-qisṭ** | Justice against the self, against parents, against relatives — without exception for relationships. The justice-command is unconditional. Following desire (`hawā`) causes deviation. The instruction is: be a standing-for-justice person even when the verdict goes against those you love. |
| **Ayah 69: The elevated company** | Those who obey Allah and the Messenger are placed in the company of: prophets → ṣiddīqūn → martyrs → ṣāliḥīn. The obedience connects the ordinary believer to the highest-tier community. The company one keeps in the Hereafter is determined by one's orientation in dunya. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Nafsin wāḥida social architecture: all human kinship is the extension of the single-soul origin | ❌ Missing |
| Tower-building futility: no fortification solves the death-problem — security-seeking misidentifies the problem | ❌ Missing |
| Unconditional justice: justice-standing is against the self too — hawā-following is the deviation-cause | ❌ Missing |
| Company-elevation through obedience: orientation determines Hereafter-company | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 92 — Surah Al-Ḥadīd (57) — Iron; whatever is in the heavens and earth glorifies Allah; He is the First and the Last and the Apparent and the Hidden; He knows what enters the earth and what comes out of it; He is with you wherever you are; "believe in Allah and His Messenger and spend from what He has made you trustees of (`mimmā ja'alakum mustakhlafīna fīh`)"; the light of the believers running before them; the life of this world is play and amusement and adornment and boasting; We sent down iron in which is great military might and benefits for people.*

---

### REVELATION 92 — SURAH AL-ḤADĪD (57), ALL 29 AYAT
*Iron — al-Awwal/al-Ākhir/al-Ẓāhir/al-Bāṭin (four paired divine names); He is with you wherever you are; trustees-stewardship spending; the believer's light running before them; dunya's five-stage life-description; We sent down iron; monasticism innovated by humans — we did not prescribe it.*

---

**Ayah 3: Four paired names:**
> 3. **"He is the First (`al-Awwal`) and the Last (`al-Ākhir`) and the Manifest (`al-Ẓāhir`) and the Hidden (`al-Bāṭin`) — and He is knowing of all things"**

**Ayah 4: With you wherever:**
> 4. "He knows what enters the earth and what comes out of it and what descends from the sky and what ascends into it — **and He is with you wherever you are (`wa-huwa ma'akum ayna mā kuntum`) — and Allah is of what you do seeing"**

**Ayah 7: Trustees of what was given:**
> 7. **"Believe in Allah and His Messenger and spend from what He has made you trustees of (`mimmā ja'alakum mustakhlafīna fīh`) — for those among you who believe and spend — for them is a great reward"**

**Ayah 20: Dunya's five stages:**
> 20. **"Know that the life of this world is play (`la'ib`) and amusement (`lahw`) and adornment (`zīna`) and boasting among yourselves (`tafākhur`) and competition in increase of wealth and children — like a rain whose plant growth pleases the farmers — then it dries and you see it yellowed — then it becomes debris — and in the Hereafter is severe punishment and forgiveness from Allah and approval — and what is the worldly life except the enjoyment of delusion"**

**Ayah 25: Iron sent down:**
> 25. **"We sent down iron (`anzalnā al-ḥadīd`) — in it is great military might (`ba'sun shadīd`) and benefits for people"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayah 3: Four paired divine names** | Al-Awwal/al-Ākhir (time-axis: before all beginnings, after all endings) + al-Ẓāhir/al-Bāṭin (presence-axis: more apparent than everything apparent, more hidden than everything hidden). Four names covering all dimensions: temporal and spatial. The source is at both extremes of every axis simultaneously. |
| **Ayah 4: Ma'akum ayna mā kuntum** | "With you wherever you are." Not watching from a distance — with you. The companionship-declaration. The source's being-with is universal and unbroken — no location is outside it. The soul that feels alone is not outside the presence — it has lost the perception of the presence. |
| **Ayah 7: Mustakhlafīna fīh** | "Trustees of what He gave you." Wealth is not owned — it is a trust. The believer is a steward (`mustakhlaf`) not an owner. Spending from it is returning the trust to its intended circulation. Hoarding the trust is the trustee refusing the stewardship. |
| **Ayah 20: Five-stage dunya arc** | Play → amusement → adornment → boasting → competition. Then: rain → plant growth (farmers pleased) → yellowing → drying → debris. Dunya moves through exactly these five stages for every soul. The rain-metaphor shows the arc: freshness → growth-pleasure → decay → nothing. The soul that stays at the growth-pleasure stage forgets the debris-end. |
| **Ayah 25: Iron sent down** | `Anzalnā al-ḥadīd` — We sent down iron. Iron is described as sent from the sky (`anzalnā` = descended). This is the language of provision-descent — the same verb used for Quran and rain. Material resources are not self-existing — they are sent-down provision. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Four-name axis coverage: al-Awwal/Ākhir + Ẓāhir/Bāṭin covers all temporal and presence dimensions | ❌ Missing |
| Ma'akum-perception: the source is with every soul always — aloneness is a perception-loss, not a reality | ❌ Missing |
| Mustakhlaf-stewardship: wealth is a trust to circulate, not property to hoard | ❌ Missing |
| Five-stage dunya arc: every dunya-attachment follows the play→debris arc | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 93 — Surah Muḥammad (47) — The Prophet; those who disbelieve and block from the path of Allah — He will nullify their deeds; those who believe and do righteous deeds and believe in what was sent down to Muḥammad — He will remove their misdeeds and improve their condition; have they not traveled in the earth and seen the outcome of those who were before them?; "do not weaken and call for peace while you are superior"; the description of Paradise; the life of this world is play and amusement.*

---

### REVELATION 93 — SURAH MUḤAMMAD (47), ALL 38 AYAT
*The Prophet — nullified deeds vs. removed misdeeds; if you support Allah He will support you and make your feet firm; the deeds-nullification by turning back; Paradise's rivers of water/milk/wine/honey; test of hearts through hardship; "if you turn away He will replace you with another people."*

---

**Ayah 7: The naṣr-exchange:**
> 7. **"O you who believe — if you support Allah (`in tanṣurū Allāh`) — He will support you and make your feet firm"**

**Ayah 12: Description of Paradise:**
> 12. **"Indeed Allah will admit those who believe and do righteous deeds to gardens beneath which rivers flow — and those who disbelieve enjoy themselves and eat as cattle eat — and the Fire is their residence"**

**Ayah 15: Four rivers of Paradise:**
> 15. **"The description of the Paradise promised to the muttaqīn: in it are rivers of water untainted — rivers of milk whose taste never changes — rivers of wine delicious to those who drink — rivers of purified honey — and in it for them are all fruits and forgiveness from their Lord"**

**Ayah 31: The test reveals what is inside:**
> 31. **"We will certainly test you until We make evident those who strive among you and the patient — and We will test your news (character)"**

**Ayah 38: Replace with another people:**
> 38. **"Here you are — invited to spend in the cause of Allah — but among you are those who are stingy — and whoever is stingy is only stingy against himself — Allah is free of need and you are the needy ones — and if you turn away He will replace you with another people — then they will not be like you"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayah 7: Naṣr-exchange** | "If you support Allah — He will support you." The support is conditional and structural: your action (naṣr) → His action (naṣr + tathbīt). The sequence is human-first. The source's support is activated by the human's engagement. The soul that waits for support before engaging misunderstands the sequence. |
| **Ayah 15: Four rivers** | Paradise's rivers are categorized by substance: water (pure) + milk (unchanging taste) + wine (delicious-to-drinkers) + honey (purified). Four distinct categories of provision — each with a defining quality. The provision of Paradise is differentiated, not uniform. |
| **Ayah 31: Test-to-reveal** | The test's purpose is `li-na'lama al-mujāhidīna minkum wa-al-ṣābirīn` — to make evident the strivers and the patient. The test reveals what is inside — it does not create new qualities. The soul's pre-existing character becomes manifest through trial. Testing is a revelation-mechanism, not a punishment-mechanism. |
| **Ayah 38: You are the needy ones** | "Allah is free of need and you are the needy ones" (`wa-Allāhu al-ghanī wa-antumu al-fuqarā'`). The soul that withholds spending withholds from itself — it damages its own neediness-relationship with the source. The stingy one is stingy against himself. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Naṣr-sequence: human naṣr-engagement activates divine naṣr — the human moves first | ❌ Missing |
| Test-as-revelation: trials reveal pre-existing character — they do not create new qualities | ❌ Missing |
| Fuqarā' recognition: acknowledging need is the correct orientation — the needy relationship with the source is proper | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 94 — Surah Al-Ra'd (13) — The Thunder; Alif-Lam-Mīm-Rā'; He raises the sky without visible pillars — then He settled over the Throne — He subjected the sun and moon; He spread the earth and placed on it firmly anchored mountains; the thunder glorifies His praise; "indeed Allah does not change the condition of a people until they change what is in themselves"; the example of those who answered their Lord and those who did not — like one who opens his hands to water reaching his mouth but it does not reach it.*

---

### REVELATION 94 — SURAH AL-RA'D (13), ALL 43 AYAT
*The Thunder — the sky without pillars; thunder glorifying; the change-law: condition doesn't change until self changes; "the good word is like a good tree"; the example of truth vs. falsehood (froth disappears, what benefits remains); those who fulfill the covenant and those who break it.*

---

**Ayah 11: The change-law:**
> 11. **"Indeed Allah does not change the condition of a people until they change what is in themselves (`ḥattā yughayyirū mā bi-anfusihim`) — and when Allah intends harm for a people there is no repelling it — and there is for them no protector besides Him"**

**Ayah 13: Thunder glorifies:**
> 13. "The thunder glorifies His praise and the angels in awe of Him — and He sends thunderbolts and strikes with them whom He wills"

**Ayah 17: Froth perishes — what benefits remains:**
> 17. **"He sends water from the sky and valleys flow according to their capacity — and the flood carries a rising foam — and from what they heat in fire seeking ornaments or goods is a similar foam — thus Allah presents the example of truth and falsehood: as for the foam — it goes away as waste — but as for what benefits people — it remains in the earth — thus Allah presents examples"**

**Ayah 29: The tree of the good word:**
> 29. "Those who believed and whose hearts find peace in the remembrance of Allah — **indeed in the remembrance of Allah hearts find peace (`alā bi-dhikri Allāhi taṭma'inn al-qulūb`)"**

**Ayat 19–21: Those who fulfill the covenant:**
> 19–21. "Is one who knows that what was sent to you from your Lord is truth like one who is blind? — only those of understanding take heed — those who fulfill the covenant of Allah and do not break the contract — those who join what Allah has commanded to be joined — and fear their Lord — and fear the evil of the account"

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayah 11: The change-law** | The condition of a people is locked in place until the inner-change happens. External change without inner change does not shift the condition. This is the deepest Y Theory pattern: `mā bi-anfusihim` (what is in themselves) is the change-variable. The social, economic, and political condition is a downstream consequence of the inner state. |
| **Ayah 17: Froth perishes — benefit remains** | The foam image: flood and metal-heating both produce foam. The foam is visible, impressive, apparently substantial — but it disappears. `Fa-ammā al-zabad fa-yadhhabu jufā'an` (the foam goes as waste). What benefits people — the water itself, the metal itself — `famakth fī al-arḍ` — it stays in the earth. Truthfulness and benefit are the metrics of permanence. |
| **Ayah 28: Taṭma'inn al-qulūb** | Hearts find peace in the dhikr of Allah. This is a structural declaration: `alā` (indeed, truly) — the peace of the heart is found in the source's remembrance. Not in security, wealth, health, success — in dhikr. The soul that seeks peace in any other place is searching in the wrong category. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Change-law: external conditions change only when inner-self changes — inner is the change-variable | ❌ Missing |
| Froth-permanence metric: what benefits others remains; what is only impressive-appearance vanishes | ❌ Missing |
| Taṭma'inn source: peace is structurally in dhikr — all other peace-sources are incomplete substitutes | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 95 — Surah Al-Raḥmān (55) — The Most Merciful; "Al-Raḥmān — taught the Quran — created the human — taught him eloquent speech"; the sun and moon by precise calculation; the sky He raised it and set the balance; "so which of your Lord's favors will you two deny?"; two gardens for those who fear their Lord; below those two — two more gardens; the Majestic Lord blessed is He.*

---

### REVELATION 95 — SURAH AL-RAḤMĀN (55), ALL 78 AYAT
*The Most Merciful — the four-teaching-sequence: Raḥmān → Quran → human → bayān; the balance-keeping command; "fa-bi-ayyi ālā'i rabbikumā tukadhdhibān" (repeated 31 times); four gardens; the Majestic Lord who is blessed.*

---

**Ayat 1–4: The four-teaching sequence:**
> 1–4. **"Al-Raḥmān — taught the Quran (`'allama al-Qur'ān`) — created the human (`khalaqa al-insān`) — taught him eloquent speech (`'allamahu al-bayān`)"**

**Ayat 5–7: Precision and balance:**
> 5–7. "The sun and the moon by precise calculation (`bi-ḥusbān`) — and the stars and the trees prostrate — and the sky He raised it and set the balance (`al-mīzān`)"

**Ayah 9: The balance-command:**
> 9. **"And maintain the weight with justice (`al-wazna bi-al-qisṭ`) and do not fall short in the balance"**

**Ayah 13: The 31-times refrain:**
> 13 (and 31 repetitions). **"So which of your Lord's favors will you two deny? (`fa-bi-ayyi ālā'i rabbikumā tukadhdhibān`)"**

**Ayat 46–76: Four gardens:**
> 46–47. **"And for whoever fears the standing before his Lord are two gardens"**
> 62–63. "And below those two are two more gardens"

**Ayah 78: The closing:**
> 78. **"Blessed be the name of your Lord (`tabāraka ismu rabbika`) — the Majestic, the Generous"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayat 1–4: Raḥmān-Quran-Human-Bayān** | The source (Al-Raḥmān) → action (taught Quran) → recipient (created human) → gift (taught bayān/speech). The sequence: the Most Merciful's first named act is teaching — not punishing, not judging. The human is created between two teachings: the Quran given to guide and the bayān given to express. The human is the recipient of both revelation and language. |
| **Ayah 13: 31-times refrain** | The refrain is asked 31 times across 78 verses — once for almost every two verses. The repetition is structural: each time a favor is described, the question immediately follows. The rhetorical function: "you cannot deny this one, or this one, or this one." The accumulation of undeniable favors makes denial impossible if the witness is honest. |
| **Ayat 46 + 62: Two pairs of gardens** | Four gardens for the one who fears the standing. The first two are described in elaborate detail. The second two are also described — different, not lesser. The gradations of Paradise are multi-tiered — not one uniform reward but differentiated levels of good. |
| **Ayah 7–9: Mīzān — cosmic balance** | The sky is raised and the balance (`mīzān`) is set. The cosmos operates by balance. The command to humans: maintain weight with justice, do not fall short. The cosmic balance is mirrored in the social/economic balance — what is required in the heavens is required on earth. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Raḥmān-teaching-sequence: the first divine act toward humans is teaching — not commanding | ❌ Missing |
| 31-times structure: the impossibility of denial is built through accumulated undeniable-favor testimony | ❌ Missing |
| Mīzān-mirroring: cosmic balance → social/economic justice is the same principle at different scales | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 96 — Surah Al-Insān (76) — The Human; did there come upon the human a period of time when he was nothing worth mentioning?; We created the human from a mixed sperm-drop — We made him hearing and seeing; We showed him the way — whether he is grateful or ungrateful; indeed We have prepared for the disbelievers chains and shackles and a blazing fire; indeed the righteous will drink from a cup with camphor; they fulfill their vow and fear a Day whose evil is widespread.*

---

### REVELATION 96 — SURAH AL-INSĀN (76), ALL 31 AYAT
*The Human — the pre-existence period of non-mention; hearing-and-seeing given; the way shown (either grateful or ungrateful); the righteous's feeding of the poor and orphan and captive "for the face of Allah only — we want from you no reward and no gratitude"; the three-gift profile of the righteous in Paradise.*

---

**Ayat 1–3: The origin and the choice:**
> 1–3. **"Did there not come upon the human a period of time — when he was not a thing mentioned? — We created the human from a mixed sperm-drop — to test him — We made him hearing and seeing — We guided him to the way — whether grateful or ungrateful (`immā shākirān wa-immā kafūrā`)"**

**Ayat 8–9: Feeding for the face of Allah:**
> 8–9. **"They give food in spite of their love for it — to the poor and the orphan and the captive — (saying): `innamā nuṭ'imukum li-wajhi Allāh` — we feed you only for the face of Allah — we desire from you no reward and no gratitude"**

**Ayah 22–23: The reward:**
> 22–23. "Indeed this is for you a reward — and your striving has been appreciated — We revealed to you the Quran as a gradual revelation"

**Ayah 30: The will-within-will:**
> 30. **"And you do not will except that Allah wills — indeed Allah is Knowing and Wise"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayah 1: The non-mention period** | "A period of time when he was not a thing mentioned." Before creation the soul was literally `lam yakun shay'an madhkūrā` (not a thing worth mentioning). The beginning of the human story is absolute non-existence. This is the foundation: existence itself is a gift — the baseline is absence. |
| **Ayah 3: Immā shākirān immā kafūrā** | "Either grateful or ungrateful." The way is shown — then the choice is binary. The two options are gratitude (`shukr`) and ingratitude (`kufr`). The path is clear. The human has hearing and seeing for this exact purpose: to receive the way and choose. |
| **Ayah 9: Li-wajhi Allāh** | "For the face of Allah only." The disinterested action — feeding without expecting return from the receiver. The purest form of action: `lā nurīdu minkum jazā'an wa-lā shukūrā` — we want from you no reward and no thanks. The action is directed vertically (toward the face of Allah) not horizontally (toward the receiver's gratitude). |
| **Ayah 30: Will-within-will** | "You do not will except that Allah wills." Human will is real but nested within divine will. The human genuinely chooses — and the source's will encompasses all human choosing. This is not compulsion — it is the architecture of embedded will. Free will and divine will are not in conflict: the human's will operates inside the divine will's permission-space. |

---

**System gaps:**

| Gap | Status |
|---|---|
| Non-mention baseline: existence is a gift — the pre-existence baseline is absolute non-mention | ❌ Missing |
| Li-wajhi Allāh action: vertical-directed action (for the source's face) that does not seek horizontal-return | ❌ Missing |
| Will-within-will architecture: human will is real and embedded within divine will — not contradiction but nesting | ❌ Missing |

---

*Next: Revelation 97 — Surah Al-Ṭalāq (65) — Divorce; O Prophet — when you divorce women divorce them for their waiting period and count the waiting period — and fear Allah your Lord; those who fear Allah — He will make a way out for them — and will provide for them from where they did not expect; whoever relies on Allah — He is sufficient for him — indeed Allah will accomplish His purpose — He has already set for everything a decreed extent (`qadar`).*

---

### REVELATION 97 — SURAH AL-ṬALĀQ (65), ALL 12 AYAT
*Divorce — the tawakkul-provision sequence: taqwā → makhraj (way out) + rizq from unexpected; qadar-everything; whoever relies on Allah — He is sufficient; Allah's command will be accomplished.*

---

**Ayat 2–3: The taqwā-provision sequence:**
> 2–3. **"Whoever fears Allah — He will make a way out for him (`yaj'al lahu makhrajā`) — and will provide for him from where he did not expect (`wa-yarzuqhu min ḥaythu lā yaḥtasib`) — and whoever relies upon Allah — then He is sufficient for him — indeed Allah will accomplish His purpose — Allah has already set for everything a decreed extent"**

**Ayah 5: The qadar-declaration:**
> 5. **"That is the command of Allah — He has sent it down to you — and whoever fears Allah — He will remove from him his misdeeds and make his reward great"**

---

**Y Theory / Pattern language:**

| Section | Pattern translation |
|---|---|
| **Ayat 2–3: The three-step taqwā-outcome chain** | Taqwā → makhraj (exit/way-out from situations with no apparent exit) → rizq min ḥaythu lā yaḥtasib (provision from an unexpected direction). The sequence is structural: taqwā is the input, makhraj and unexpected-provision are the outputs. The soul that has taqwā does not need to know the exit — the exit is generated. |
| **Ayah 3: Tawakkul sufficiency** | "Whoever relies upon Allah — He is sufficient for him." This is the strongest sufficiency-claim: unconditional, without qualification. The condition is only `tawakkul` — genuine reliance. When that reliance is real, the source's sufficiency activates without limit. |
| **Qadar: Everything has a decreed extent** | `Qad ja'ala Allāhu li-kulli shay'in qadrā` — for everything a measure.
